# Canonical MCP Consolidated Validation (2026-03-28)

This is the single consolidated view for the BNY extracted graph. It shows, in one place, how extracted documents, entities, events, relationships, and properties map to the validated MCP interpretation.

This file supersedes the need to cross-read these narrower helper docs for most questions:

- `design/canonical-mcp-entity-validation-2026-03-28.md`
- `design/canonical-mcp-event-validation-2026-03-28.md`
- `design/extracted-graph-full-inventory-2026-03-28.md`

Status values:

- `resolved_to_neid`: extracted item exists under its own canonical NEID in the validated MCP view
- `merged_into_neid`: extracted item is accounted for through entity resolution and maps to a different canonical NEID/name
- `seed_only_current_id`: current rebuilt snapshot still exposes only a seed ID for the extracted item
- `not_resolved`: no canonical ID was confirmed from current local evidence

- Use this file when the question is: "What did this extracted thing map to in the validated MCP view?"
